Vēnātōrēs, cum aliter eum captāre nōn possint, illam arborem sīc incīdunt ut elephantus dormiēns illam frangat et cadat? According to the passage, how does an elephant sleep? ANSWER:BY RECLINING / RESTING / APPLYING ITSELF TO A TREE BONUS: What is the method described for catching elephants? ANSWER:THE TREE (UPON WHICH THE ELEPHANT IS RESTING) SHOULD BE CUT INTO IN SUCH A WAY THAT THE ELEPHANT BREAKS THE TREE AND FALLS DOWN BONUS: When do hunters use this method? ANSWER:WHEN OTHER METHODS FAIL, WHEN THEY CANNOT OTHERWISE CAPTURE THE ELEPHANT
